!Series_title	"DNA methylation profiling of the Biomarkers of Aging Consortium Cohort"
!Series_geo_accession	"GSE246337"
!Series_status	"Public on May 29 2024"
!Series_submission_date	"Oct 26 2023"

!Series_web_link	"https://www.biorxiv.org/content/10.1101/2024.05.30.596713v1.full"
!Series_summary	"We generated DNA methylation profiles of 500 diverse individuals to enable to construction and validation of DNA methylation biomarkers of aging."
!Series_overall_design	"We selected 500 subjects to generate a cohort that was evenly divided between male and female, and represented a broad range of ages and race/ethnicity. DNA isolated from the blood of these subjects was profiled with the Illumina Infinium MethylationEPIC v2.0 array."
